<pr_description>
Content Dialog - need update the overlay
### Current behavior 🐛

When open a Content Dialog with the App restored, and maximize, the overlay is not corret.
And after restore again it is not on the correct position.

![Image](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/33139e40-c820-4259-a2ce-a8a024d1c183)


### Expected behavior 🎯

Overlay use the full window when resize (maximize).
Content Dialog stay centralized when restore.

### How to reproduce it (as minimally and precisely as possible) 🔬

Create a new UnoApp Blank

> dotnet new unoapp -o SampleTestVSCodeDev 

Add a Button to the Main Page.
```xaml
<Button Content="Click" Click="Button_Click" />
```

Add a dialog on the backend

```csharp


    private async Task Button_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
    {
        var dialog = new ContentDialog
        {
            Title = "Hello World",
            Content = "This is a sample dialog.",
            CloseButtonText = "Close",
            XamlRoot = this.XamlRoot,
        };
        await dialog.ShowAsync();
    }
```

Or use this project

[SampleTestVSCodeDev.zip](https://github.com/user-attachments/files/20836875/SampleTestVSCodeDev.zip)

Run the App.
Click the button (dialog will open)
Maximize (overlay will break)
Restore (Dialog is not centralized)


See video

https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/539d5947-1d5d-45a7-9945-47152a8df890

     4			private void SizeAndPositionContentInPopup()
     5			{
     6				var m_tpPopup = _popup;
     7	
     8				double xOffset = 0;
     9				double yOffset = 0;
    10	
    11				if (XamlRoot is null)
    12				{
    13					if (this is not MessageDialogContentDialog)
    14					{
    15						throw new InvalidOperationException(
    16							"Trying to set position of the dialog before it is associated with a visual tree. " +
    17							"This can happen if the dialog's XamlRoot was not set.");
    18					}
    19					else
    20					{
    21						throw new InvalidOperationException(
    22							"Trying to set position of the dialog before it is associated with a visual tree. " +
    23							"Make sure to use InitializeWithWindow before calling ShowAsync.");
    24					}
    25				}
    26	
    27	#if !HAS_UNO
    28				var xamlRootSize = XamlRoot.Size;
    29	#else
    30				var xamlRootSize = XamlRoot.VisualTree.TrueVisibleBounds.Size;
    31	#endif
    32	
    33				var flowDirection = FlowDirection;
    34	
    35				FrameworkElement spBackgroundAsFE = m_tpBackgroundElementPart;
    36	
    37				// Uno note: we're using latest template version (Redstone3). For now we're not supporting legacy templates.
    38	
    39				if (m_placementMode == PlacementMode.EntireControlInPopup)
    40				{
    41					Height = xamlRootSize.Height;
    42					Width = xamlRootSize.Width;
    43				}
    44				else if (m_tpLayoutRootPart != null)

    46					m_tpLayoutRootPart.Height = xamlRootSize.Height;
    47					m_tpLayoutRootPart.Width = xamlRootSize.Width;
    48				}

    50				// Uno - omitted code related to display regions, which aren't currently supported
    51	
    52				// When the ContentDialog is in the visual tree, the popup offset has added
    53				// to it the top-left point of where layout measured and arranged it to.
    54				// Since we want ContentDialog to be an overlay, we need to subtract off that
    55				// point in order to ensure the ContentDialog is always being displayed in
    56				// window coordinates instead of local coordinates.
    57				if (m_placementMode == PlacementMode.TransplantedRootInPopup)
    58				{
    59					GeneralTransform transformToRoot = m_tpPopup.TransformToVisual(null);
    60					var offsetFromRoot = (transformToRoot.TransformPoint(default));
    61	
    62					{
    63						xOffset =
    64							flowDirection == FlowDirection.LeftToRight ?
    65							(xOffset - offsetFromRoot.X) :
    66							(xOffset - offsetFromRoot.X) * -1;
    67					}
    68	
    69					yOffset -= offsetFromRoot.Y;
    70				}
    71	
    72				// Set the ContentDialog left and top position.
    73				m_tpPopup.HorizontalOffset = xOffset;

    17	namespace Microsoft.UI.Xaml.Controls
    18	{
    19		internal partial class ContentDialogPopupPanel : PopupPanel
    20		{
    21			public ContentDialogPopupPanel(ContentDialog dialog) : base(dialog._popup)
    22			{
    23			}
    24	
    25			protected override Size MeasureOverride(Size availableSize)
    26			{
    27				var actualAvailableSize = CalculateDialogAvailableSize(availableSize);
    28				return base.MeasureOverride(actualAvailableSize);
    29			}
    30	
    31			protected override Size ArrangeOverride(Size finalSize)
    32			{
    33				if (this.Log().IsEnabled(Uno.Foundation.Logging.LogLevel.Debug))
    34				{
    35					this.Log().LogDebug($"ArrangeOverride ContentDialogPopupPanel {finalSize}");
    36				}
    37	
    38				foreach (var child in Children)
    39				{
    40					if (!(child is UIElement elem))
    41					{
    42						continue;
    43					}
    44	
    45					var desiredSize = elem.DesiredSize;
    46					var rect = CalculateDialogPlacement(desiredSize, finalSize);
    47	
    48					if (this.Log().IsEnabled(Uno.Foundation.Logging.LogLevel.Debug))
    49					{
    50						this.Log().LogDebug($"Arranging ContentDialogPopupPanel {desiredSize} to {rect}");
    51					}
    52	
    53					elem.Arrange(rect);
    54				}
    55	
    56				return finalSize;
    57			}
    58	
    59			private Size CalculateDialogAvailableSize(Size availableSize)
    60			{
    61				// Skip calculation if in the context of Uno Islands.
    62				if (!CoreApplication.IsFullFledgedApp)
    63				{
    64					return availableSize;
    65				}
    66	
    67				var visibleBounds = XamlRoot?.VisualTree.TrueVisibleBounds ?? default;
    68	
    69				if (availableSize.Width > visibleBounds.Width)
    70				{
    71					availableSize.Width = visibleBounds.Width;
    72				}
    73				if (availableSize.Height > visibleBounds.Height)
    74				{
    75					availableSize.Height = visibleBounds.Height;
    76				}
    77	
    78				return availableSize;
    79			}
    80	
    81			private Rect CalculateDialogPlacement(Size desiredSize, Size finalSize)
    82			{
    83				Rect visibleBounds = XamlRoot?.VisualTree.TrueVisibleBounds ?? default;
    84	
    85				var maximumWidth = Math.Min(visibleBounds.Width, finalSize.Width);
    86				var maximumHeight = Math.Min(visibleBounds.Height, finalSize.Height);
    87	
    88				// Make sure the desiredSize fits in visibleBounds
    89				var actualWidth = Math.Min(desiredSize.Width, maximumWidth);
    90				var actualHeight = Math.Min(desiredSize.Height, maximumHeight);
    91	
    92				var xOffset = Math.Max((maximumWidth - actualWidth) / 2, visibleBounds.X);
    93				var yOffset = Math.Max((maximumHeight - actualHeight) / 2, visibleBounds.Y);
    94	
    95				var finalRect = new Rect(
    96					xOffset,
    97					yOffset,
    98					actualWidth,
    99					actualHeight
   100				);
   101	
   102				return finalRect;
   103			}
   104

   106			// a second Popup containing a stretched Rectangle. To keep things simple, we just block pointers from passing from here.
   107			internal override bool IsViewHit() => true;
   108		}

    76					}

    78	
    79					// TODO: support in-place
    80					m_placementMode = PlacementMode.EntireControlInPopup;

    83					EnsureTemplate();
    84					if (HasValidAppliedTemplate())
    85					{
    86						PrepareContent();
    87					}
    88	
    89					_popup.Child = this;
    90
